Maven Pro Regular (MavenPro-Regular.ttf)

name

MS NID 6

MS NID 6, PostScript Name check for illegal characters.
Monotype uses NID 6 for creating CSS classes for their demo HTML. The following characters cause issues in the CSS code: '
, , , &, _, [, ], (, ), {, }, <, >, /, \, %'

NID 6 is 'MavenPro-Regular', Everything looks good.

Maven Pro Medium Regular (MavenPro-Medium.ttf)

name

MS NID 16/17

MS NID 16 + NID 17 should match NID 1 (+2).
Otherwise cross platform compatibility does not work between Mac (uses NID 16+17) and Windows (uses NID 1+2). (Jan 2019)

NID 16 'Maven Pro' + 'Space' + NID 17 'Medium' = NID 1 'Maven Pro Medium'.

Maven Pro Bold (MavenPro-Bold.ttf)

name

MS NID 6

MS NID 6, PostScript Name check for illegal characters.
Monotype uses NID 6 for creating CSS classes for their demo HTML. The following characters cause issues in the CSS code: '

NID 6 is 'MavenPro-Bold', Everything looks good.

name

MS NID 6

MS NID 6, PostScript Name check for illegal characters.
Monotype uses NID 6 for creating CSS classes for their demo HTML. The following characters cause issues in the CSS code: '
, , , &, _, [, ], (, ), {, }, <, >, /, \, %'

NID 6 is 'MavenPro-Black', Everything looks good.

Maven Pro Black Regular (MavenPro-Black.ttf)

name

MS NID 16/17

MS NID 16 + NID 17 should match NID 1 (+2).
Otherwise cross platform compatibility does not work between Mac (uses NID 16+17) and Windows (uses NID 1+2). (Jan 2019)

NID 16 'Maven Pro' + 'Space' + NID 17 'Black' = NID 1 'Maven Pro Black'.

kern

'kern' table and 'GPOS' kerning.

Font has GPOS kerning and no 'kern' table.
Verify with the spec or PM what is required.

gasp

Default

gasp table default is:
Grid-fit = True, Do gray = True, Symmetric grid-fit = True, Symmetric smoothing = True
and should be:
Grid-fit = True, Do gray = True, Symmetric grid-fit = True, Symmetric smoothing = True

PostScript names

Every PostScript name is fine.
